━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
14. CODE QUALITY MARKERS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

▓▓▓ Detects: TODO, FIXME, HACK, XXX, NOTE
Technical debt markers indicate incomplete or problematic code.
  ✓ OK No technical debt markers

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
15. REGEX & STRING SAFETY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

▓▓▓ Detects: ReDoS, dynamic regex with input, escaping issues
Regex bugs cause performance issues and security vulnerabilities.

• Nested quantifiers (ReDoS risk)

• Dynamic re.compile from variables

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
16. I/O & RESOURCE SAFETY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

▓▓▓ Detects: open without with, missing encoding, rmtree(ignore_errors)
I/O bugs leak resources and produce nondeterministic behavior.

• open(...) without context manager
  ✓ OK File usage appears context-managed

• open() without explicit encoding

• shutil.rmtree(ignore_errors=True)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
17. TYPING STRICTNESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

▓▓▓ Detects: Any usage, type: ignore density
Type hygiene reduces runtime errors.

• 'Any' usage

• type: ignore comments

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
18. PYTHON I/O & MODULE USAGE
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

▓▓▓ Detects: os.system, wildcard imports, dynamic import
Prefer safer subprocess APIs and explicit imports.

• os.system invocations

• Dynamic imports

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
19. RESOURCE LIFECYCLE CORRELATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

▓▓▓ Detects: File handles, subprocesses, and async tasks missing cleanup
Unreleased resources leak descriptors, zombie processes, and pending tasks

• Resource lifecycle correlation
  ✓ OK All tracked resource acquisitions have matching cleanups

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
